# .resources

Keyword: .suggestions

Description:

* Retrieve nested suggestions of UniqueBible App commands.
* This command keyword takes no parameter.
* This command output in JSON format only with all UniqueBible App web API endpoints: `/html`, `/json`, `/plain`.
* This command applies to UniqueBible App running mode `http-server` only.

# Use Case

The retrieved suggestions are useful for applications to make suggestions as users enter UniqueBible App commands.

As an example, we implemented this in [ToolMate AI](https://github.com/eliranwong/toolmate):

![suggestions](https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/2ff21552-2c2c-4bde-9b0f-4505e72ea038)

# Command Format

.suggestions

# Example

Command: `.suggestions`

URL: https://bible.gospelchurch.uk/json?cmd=.suggestions

Output:

